\doxysection{rlgl.\+h}
\hypertarget{rlgl_8h_source}{}\label{rlgl_8h_source}\index{cmake-\/build-\/debug/vcpkg\_installed/x64-\/windows/include/rlgl.h@{cmake-\/build-\/debug/vcpkg\_installed/x64-\/windows/include/rlgl.h}}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{/**********************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ rlgl\ v4.5\ -\/\ A\ multi-\/OpenGL\ abstraction\ layer\ with\ an\ immediate-\/mode\ style\ API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ DESCRIPTION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ An\ abstraction\ layer\ for\ multiple\ OpenGL\ versions\ (1.1,\ 2.1,\ 3.3\ Core,\ 4.3\ Core,\ ES\ 2.0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ that\ provides\ a\ pseudo-\/OpenGL\ 1.1\ immediate-\/mode\ style\ API\ (rlVertex,\ rlTranslate,\ rlRotate...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ ADDITIONAL\ NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ When\ choosing\ an\ OpenGL\ backend\ different\ than\ OpenGL\ 1.1,\ some\ internal\ buffer\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ initialized\ on\ rlglInit()\ to\ accumulate\ vertex\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ When\ an\ internal\ state\ change\ is\ required\ all\ the\ stored\ vertex\ data\ is\ renderer\ in\ batch,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ additionally,\ rlDrawRenderBatchActive()\ could\ be\ called\ to\ force\ flushing\ of\ the\ batch.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Some\ resources\ are\ also\ loaded\ for\ convenience,\ here\ the\ complete\ list:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ batch\ (RLGL.defaultBatch):\ RenderBatch\ system\ to\ accumulate\ vertex\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ texture\ (RLGL.defaultTextureId):\ 1x1\ white\ pixel\ R8G8B8A8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ shader\ (RLGL.State.defaultShaderId,\ RLGL.State.defaultShaderLocs)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Internal\ buffer\ (and\ resources)\ must\ be\ manually\ unloaded\ calling\ rlglClose().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ CONFIGURATION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_11}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_21}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_33}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_43}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_ES2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_ES3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Use\ selected\ OpenGL\ graphics\ backend,\ should\ be\ supported\ by\ platform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Those\ preprocessor\ defines\ are\ only\ used\ on\ rlgl\ module,\ if\ OpenGL\ version\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ required\ by\ any\ other\ module,\ use\ rlGetVersion()\ to\ check\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RLGL\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Generates\ the\ implementation\ of\ the\ library\ into\ the\ included\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ not\ defined,\ the\ library\ is\ in\ header\ only\ mode\ and\ can\ be\ included\ in\ other\ headers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ or\ source\ files\ without\ problems.\ But\ only\ ONE\ file\ should\ hold\ the\ implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RLGL\_RENDER\_TEXTURES\_HINT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Enable\ framebuffer\ objects\ (fbo)\ support\ (enabled\ by\ default)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Some\ GPUs\ could\ not\ support\ them\ despite\ the\ OpenGL\ version}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RLGL\_SHOW\_GL\_DETAILS\_INFO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Show\ OpenGL\ extensions\ and\ capabilities\ detailed\ logs\ on\ init}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RLGL\_ENABLE\_OPENGL\_DEBUG\_CONTEXT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Enable\ debug\ context\ (only\ available\ on\ OpenGL\ 4.3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ rlgl\ capabilities\ could\ be\ customized\ just\ defining\ some\ internal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ values\ before\ library\ inclusion\ (default\ values\ listed):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_BATCH\_BUFFER\_ELEMENTS\ \ \ 8192\ \ \ \ //\ Default\ internal\ render\ batch\ elements\ limits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_BATCH\_BUFFERS\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 1\ \ \ \ //\ Default\ number\ of\ batch\ buffers\ (multi-\/buffering)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_BATCH\_DRAWCALLS\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 256\ \ \ \ //\ Default\ number\ of\ batch\ draw\ calls\ (by\ state\ changes:\ mode,\ texture)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_BATCH\_MAX\_TEXTURE\_UNITS\ \ \ \ 4\ \ \ \ //\ Maximum\ number\ of\ textures\ units\ that\ can\ be\ activated\ on\ batch\ drawing\ (SetShaderValueTexture())}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_MAX\_MATRIX\_STACK\_SIZE\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 32\ \ \ \ //\ Maximum\ size\ of\ internal\ Matrix\ stack}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_MAX\_SHADER\_LOCATIONS\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 32\ \ \ \ //\ Maximum\ number\ of\ shader\ locations\ supported}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_CULL\_DISTANCE\_NEAR\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 0.01\ \ \ \ //\ Default\ projection\ matrix\ near\ cull\ distance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_CULL\_DISTANCE\_FAR\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 1000.0\ \ \ \ //\ Default\ projection\ matrix\ far\ cull\ distance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ When\ loading\ a\ shader,\ the\ following\ vertex\ attributes\ and\ uniform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ location\ names\ are\ tried\ to\ be\ set\ automatically:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_POSITION\ \ \ \ \ "{}vertexPosition"{}\ \ \ \ //\ Bound\ by\ default\ to\ shader\ location:\ 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_TEXCOORD\ \ \ \ \ "{}vertexTexCoord"{}\ \ \ \ //\ Bound\ by\ default\ to\ shader\ location:\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_NORMAL\ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}vertexNormal"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Bound\ by\ default\ to\ shader\ location:\ 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_COLOR\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}vertexColor"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Bound\ by\ default\ to\ shader\ location:\ 3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_TANGENT\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}vertexTangent"{}\ \ \ \ \ //\ Bound\ by\ default\ to\ shader\ location:\ 4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_TEXCOORD2\ \ \ \ "{}vertexTexCoord2"{}\ \ \ //\ Bound\ by\ default\ to\ shader\ location:\ 5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_MVP\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}mvp"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ model-\/view-\/projection\ matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_VIEW\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}matView"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ view\ matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_PROJECTION\ \ "{}matProjection"{}\ \ \ \ \ //\ projection\ matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_MODEL\ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}matModel"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ model\ matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_NORMAL\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}matNormal"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ normal\ matrix\ (transpose(inverse(matModelView))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_COLOR\ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}colDiffuse"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ color\ diffuse\ (base\ tint\ color,\ multiplied\ by\ texture\ color)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_SAMPLER2D\_NAME\_TEXTURE0\ \ "{}texture0"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ texture0\ (texture\ slot\ active\ 0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_SAMPLER2D\_NAME\_TEXTURE1\ \ "{}texture1"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ texture1\ (texture\ slot\ active\ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_SAMPLER2D\_NAME\_TEXTURE2\ \ "{}texture2"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ texture2\ (texture\ slot\ active\ 2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ DEPENDENCIES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ OpenGL\ libraries\ (depending\ on\ platform\ and\ OpenGL\ version\ selected)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ GLAD\ OpenGL\ extensions\ loading\ library\ (only\ for\ OpenGL\ 3.3\ Core,\ 4.3\ Core)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01180\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ rlRotatef(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ angle,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ x,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ y,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{01181\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01182\ \ \ \ \ Matrix\ matRotation\ =\ rlMatrixIdentity();}
\DoxyCodeLine{01183\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01184\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Axis\ vector\ (x,\ y,\ z)\ normalization}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01185\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ lengthSquared\ =\ x*x\ +\ y*y\ +\ z*z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01186\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ ((lengthSquared\ !=\ 1.0f)\ \&\&\ (lengthSquared\ !=\ 0.0f))}
\DoxyCodeLine{01187\ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01188\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ inverseLength\ =\ 1.0f/sqrtf(lengthSquared);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01189\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ x\ *=\ inverseLength;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01190\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ y\ *=\ inverseLength;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01191\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ z\ *=\ inverseLength;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01192\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01193\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01194\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Rotation\ matrix\ generation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01195\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ sinres\ =\ sinf(DEG2RAD*angle);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01196\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ cosres\ =\ cosf(DEG2RAD*angle);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01197\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ t\ =\ 1.0f\ -\/\ cosres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01198\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01199\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m0\ =\ x*x*t\ +\ cosres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01200\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m1\ =\ y*x*t\ +\ z*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01201\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m2\ =\ z*x*t\ -\/\ y*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01202\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m3\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01203\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01204\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m4\ =\ x*y*t\ -\/\ z*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01205\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m5\ =\ y*y*t\ +\ cosres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01206\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m6\ =\ z*y*t\ +\ x*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01207\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m7\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01208\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01209\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m8\ =\ x*z*t\ +\ y*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01210\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m9\ =\ y*z*t\ -\/\ x*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01211\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m10\ =\ z*z*t\ +\ cosres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01212\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m11\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01213\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01214\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m12\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01215\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m13\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01216\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m14\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01217\ \ \ \ \ matRotation.m15\ =\ 1.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01218\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01219\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NOTE:\ We\ transpose\ matrix\ with\ multiplication\ order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01220\ \ \ \ \ *RLGL.State.currentMatrix\ =\ rlMatrixMultiply(matRotation,\ *RLGL.State.currentMatrix);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01221\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01222\ }
